id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_body" class="ajax__tab_body ajax__scroll_vert"> <div id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures" class="ajax__tab_panel" style="visibility: visible;"> <div class="Features"> <span id="ctl00_ctl00_MainContent_uxProduct_uxProductTabs_ProductTabs_pnlFeatures_ProductFeatureDesc"><h2 class="entry-title"><span>KSG Kel Tec Shotgun 12 Gauge 18.5 Inch Barrel 2.75 Inch Chamber Picatinny Rails Dual Magazine Tubes Black Finish 14 Rounds</span></h2> <p><em><strong style="font-size: medium;"><span>Latest Generation with all improvements</span></strong></em></p> <h2><font style="color: #000000;"><span><span>Internal dual tube magazines holds 6 rounds of 12 gauge 3 inch shells each for a total capacity of 6+6+1 (7 per tube if using 2-3/4 inch shells). Pump action feeds from either the left or right tube. Feed side is manually selected by a lever located behind the trigger guard. Lever can be positioned in the center detent in order to easily clear the chamber without feeding another round from either magazine. Cross bolt style safety. Pump release lever is located in front of the trigger guard. Includes an under Picatinny rail and top Picatinny sight rail. Sling loops are built in and a basic sling is included. Soft rubber butt pad. Weighs 6.9 pounds with a 26.1 inch overall length.</span><br></span></font></h2> <p><font size="3">This bullpup pump-action shotgun has dual tube magazines that can hold a total of 14+1 rounds of ammunition. The KSG can only set to feed from the right or the left. Once the magazine is empty, the operator must use a manual switch to select the other magazine. This may appear at first glance to be disadvantage but for many people who live in areas where shotgun magazine capacity is limited by law, this feature, or lack of feature as the case may be, could allow them to legally possess the KSG.</font></p> <p><span>*pictured iron sights are not included</span></p> <p><span class="h1">Kel-Tec Shotgun (KSG) Video</span></p> <p><iframe src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/XwN8jHSEhCE" width="560" height="315" frameborder="0"></iframe></p> <p><iframe src="https://www.youtube.com/embed/W638QRLqUyc" width="560" height="315" frameborder="0"></iframe></p> <p><span class="h1">Kel-Tec KSG Features and Specifications</span></p> <table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="5" width="500"> <tbody> <tr> <td width="50%" align="left" valign="top"><font size="2"><strong>Gauge:</strong> 12</font></td> <td width="50%" align="left" valign="top"><font size="2"><strong>Action:</strong> Pump</font></td> </tr> <tr> <td width="50%" align="left" valign="top"><font size="2"><strong>Weight:</strong> 6.9 lbs</font></td> <td width="50%" align="left" valign="top"><font size="2"><strong>Barrel Length:</strong> 18.5"</font></td> </tr> <tr> <td width="50%" align="left" valign="top"><font size="2"><strong>Overall Length:</strong> 26"</font></td> <td width="50%" align="left" valign="top"><font size="2"><strong>Capacity: </strong>14 + 1</font></td> </tr> <tr> <td align="left" valign="top"><font size="2"><strong>Stock Material: </strong>Black Synthetic</font></td> <td align="left" valign="top"><font size="2"><strong>Finish: </strong>Black</font></td> </tr> </tbody> </table> <h1 class="main_title">KSG Update II (Factory News) <div class="news-cont"> <div class="sub_news"> <div class="date">07-11-2011</div> <div class="sub_news_description"> <p>Hello from Kel-Tec!</p> <p>We have been receiving an abnormally large number of calls pertaining specifically to seeing the KSG for sale on sites like Gunbroker.com.</p> <p>The bottom line is this: they are hoaxes. Kel-Tec has not shipped any weapons that are allowed to be sold. Up until this point all weapons shipped are for testing and evaluation purposes only and any testers caught selling a testing weapon will be dealt with on our end.</p> <p>We have personally investigated all instances of KSGs being sold online and have deemed them all to be untrue. We caution the public to be wary of these sales as they do not have the product to provide to the winner of these auctions.</p> <p>When the KSG starts shipping to distributors for resale we will make an announcement here on the site to let everyone know.</p> <p><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/darin_picures/keltec/ksg_4.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="601"><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/darin_picures/keltec/ksg_5.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="316"><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/darin_picures/keltec/ksg_3.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="113"><img src="../../../../Data/Default/Images/uploads/darin_picures/keltec/ksg_2.jpg" alt="" width="540" height="170"></p> <p>&nbsp;</p> </div> </div> </div> </h1></span></div>
